# Caller-burden ledger.
# Format: <theorem> <binder_index> <name> <category> <type-snippet>
#
# Mirrors `trust/baseline-axioms.txt` for the OTHER half of the trust
# surface — every parameter the caller of a canonical `equiv_<OP>` is
# on the hook for. The plan to discharge promise hypotheses MUST
# reduce this ledger; renaming a binder, or splitting one promise into
# several smaller ones, will show up as a non-shrinking diff and fail
# the gate.
#
# Categories: validator | state | entry | range | match | bridge |
#             bus_shape | transpile | byte_chain | loose | row |
#             instance | other
#
# Total rows: 2559
# Category bridge: 59
# Category bus_shape: 516
# Category byte_chain: 115
# Category entry: 67
# Category loose: 376
# Category match: 86
# Category other: 565
# Category range: 228
# Category row: 69
# Category state: 217
# Category transpile: 171
# Category validator: 90
#
